	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: phpstan.neon');
	$tmp = pathinfo('phpstan.neon');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('phpstan.neon')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('phpstan.neon', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}

	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): phpstan.neon');

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'e5a075f9b7e5556c0a1dda06d50d56757ad19c3e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'e5a075f9b7e5556c0a1dda06d50d56757ad19c3e') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'c2de23e62e575738a6038a9769d7bd8766b90fa3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'e5a075f9b7e5556c0a1dda06d50d56757ad19c3e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php') != '49c119bddee13d2c4cecb18b97d90690080278c8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php') !== '49c119bddee13d2c4cecb18b97d90690080278c8') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php') !== '39bc0f7878619bc157052ae250cb2a4d413e8858') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php') !== '49c119bddee13d2c4cecb18b97d90690080278c8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '7976a544d7dacbb51eabc90574e1b3d6d4417886') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '7976a544d7dacbb51eabc90574e1b3d6d4417886') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '5d84eb4fb1194467c6c6f7a069e5eeff62626828') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '7976a544d7dacbb51eabc90574e1b3d6d4417886') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/setup.min.css.php');
	writefile_22();
	if (!is_file('setup/setup.min.css.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup.min.css.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup.min.css.php') != '7154f9130bd75a4cbc9d9cbe1d525b22a1445fbb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.min.css.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup.min.css.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup.min.css.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.css.php') !== '7154f9130bd75a4cbc9d9cbe1d525b22a1445fbb') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.css.php') !== '71d4d199a120aa615e16753c7040e6dd505758c8') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup.min.css.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup.min.css.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup.min.css.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/setup.min.css.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_22();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.css.php') !== '7154f9130bd75a4cbc9d9cbe1d525b22a1445fbb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.min.css.php');
		}
	}
}
